df8 = df4.merge(df7, left_on='S_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df9 = df2.merge(df8, left_on='PS_SUPPKEY', right_on='S_SUPPKEY')
df10 = df1.merge(df9, left_on='L_SUPPKEY', right_on='PS_SUPPKEY')

df1 = partsupp[(partsupp['PS_PARTKEY'] != 15) | (partsupp['SUPPLYCOST'] >= 487.2752048627317)]
df2 = df1[['SUPPLYCOST', 'AVAILQTY', 'PS_SUPPKEY', 'P_COMMENT']]
df3 = supplier[(supplier['S_COMMENT'] != 'a') & (supplier['S_PHONE'].str.startswith('32-'))]
df4 = nation[(nation['N_COMMENT'] == 'l') & (nation['N_NAME'] == 'V') & (nation['N_NAME'] == 'V')]
df5 = region[(region['R_COMMENT'] == 'u') & (region['R_NAME'].str.startswith('A'))]
df6 = df4.merge(df5, left_on='N_REGIONKEY', right_on='R_REGIONKEY')
df7 = df3.merge(df6, left_on='S_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df8 = df2.merge(df7, left_on='PS_SUPPKEY', right_on='S_SUPPKEY')
df9 = lineitem.merge(df8, left_on='L_SUPPKEY', right_on='PS_SUPPKEY')
df10 = df9.groupby(by=['R_NAME', 'R_REGIONKEY']).agg('max', numeric_only=True)

df1 = partsupp[(partsupp['PS_PARTKEY'] < 47) & (partsupp['P_COMMENT'].str.startswith('n'))]
df2 = df1[['P_COMMENT', 'PS_SUPPKEY', 'AVAILQTY']]
df3 = supplier[['S_NATIONKEY', 'S_SUPPKEY', 'S_COMMENT']]
df4 = region[['R_REGIONKEY', 'R_COMMENT', 'R_NAME']]
df5 = nation.merge(df4, left_on='N_REGIONKEY', right_on='R_REGIONKEY')
df6 = df3.merge(df5, left_on='S_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df7 = df2.merge(df6, left_on='PS_SUPPKEY', right_on='S_SUPPKEY')
df8 = lineitem.merge(df7, left_on='L_SUPPKEY', right_on='PS_SUPPKEY')

df1 = partsupp[['PS_PARTKEY', 'PS_SUPPKEY']]
df2 = supplier[(supplier['S_COMMENT'].str.startswith('a'))]
df3 = nation[['N_COMMENT', 'N_REGIONKEY', 'N_NAME', 'N_NATIONKEY']]
df4 = region[(region['R_COMMENT'] != 'h')]
df5 = df3.merge(df4, left_on='N_REGIONKEY', right_on='R_REGIONKEY')
df6 = df2.merge(df5, left_on='S_NATIONKEY', right_on='N_NATIONKEY')
df7 = df1.merge(df6, left_on='PS_SUPPKEY', right_on='S_SUPPKEY')
df8 = lineitem.merge(df7, left_on='L_PARTKEY', right_on='PS_PARTKEY')
df9 = df8.groupby(by=['R_REGIONKEY', 'R_COMMENT', 'R_NAME']).agg('mean', numeric_only=True)
